heritage as Indian Americans,\" reads the Change.org petition to keep the Mexican Pizza on the menu.&#160;</p><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet blockquote\" data-lang=\"en\" data-cards=\"\" data-conversation=\"\">&#8212;Vinny Venkat  (@venkatinthehat) <a href=\"https://twitter.com/mims/statuses/1301657620323811328?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\">September 3, 2020</a></blockquote><script async src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet blockquote\" data-lang=\"en\" data-cards=\"\" data-conversation=\"\">&#8212;Swapna Krishna  (@skrishna) <a href=\"https://twitter.com/mims/statuses/1301615194280464384?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\">September 3, 2020</a></blockquote><script async src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><p><em><strong>Read more: </strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/franchisees-fear-lack-of-aid-could-kill-businesses-in-pandemic-2020-10\">36,000 franchisees could shutter forever without a new stimulus package, as operators of iconic brands like Pizza Hut, Golden Corral, and more file for bankruptcy</a></em></p><p>Taco Bell said that it needed to remove the Mexican Pizza from the menu to make way for new options. Ditching the Mexican Pizza also helps Taco Bell become more sustainable, as the menu item's packaging accounts for more than 7 million pounds in paperboard waste every year in the US.&#160;</p><p>\"While we know fans may be understandably sad to see some of their favorites go, this evolution of our menu truly paves the way for fresh new ideas,\" Mike Grams, Taco Bell's president and global chief operating officer, said in a statement in September. \"The creativity and innovation in our kitchen hasn't slowed down at all, and we look forward to rolling out new fan favorites.\"</p><p>2020 has been a difficult year for Taco Bell fans who are resistant to changes at the chain. Over the summer, Taco Bell slashed a number of classics from the menu, including the quesarito, the seven-layer burrito, and cheesy fiesta potatoes.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original To help, we're answering all the most common questions our readers have regarding the sales event, including dates, competing sales, how to prepare, and more.</p><h3><strong>What is Amazon Prime Day?</strong></h3><p>Introduced in 2015 in part to celebrate Amazon's 20th anniversary, the first Amazon Prime Day was a one-day-only retail holiday for Prime members that sought to overtake Black Friday as&#160;<em>the</em>&#160;sales event of the year.&#160;</p><p>During the event, prices drop to all-time lows, often beating out prices we see over Black Friday and Cyber Monday. The sale covers every product category Amazon offers: tech, beauty, home and kitchen, fashion, and smart home are just a few of the huge variety of items that will be discounted.&#160;</p><p>Last year's Amazon Prime Day was a huge success; during the 48-hour sale event held on July 15-16, Prime members bought more than 175 million items. It was the biggest shopping day in company history until it was surpassed by Cyber Monday shortly after, a familiar pattern of record-breaking.&#160;</p><h3><strong>When is Amazon Prime Day 2020?</strong></h3><p>Amazon Prime Day is scheduled for 12 a.m. PT on Tuesday, October 13 through Wednesday, October 14, 2020, as it was originally postponed due to COVID-19. Prime Day is an annual 48-hour sale where Amazon Prime members can get deals on products such as laptops, TVs, smartphones, wearables, and more.</p><p>Shoppers, however, don't need to wait until then to take advantage of deals. Prime members can shop early deals and offers leading up to Prime Day. In addition to markdowns on Amazon devices, like select Fire TVs and the Fire TV Recast, Prime members can enjoy discounts on subscriptions to <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/hz/audible/mlp/mdp/gold/annual?&_encoding=UTF8&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20-2020-20\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Audible</a>, <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/music/unlimited?ref_=assoc_tag_ph_1483579440886&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-200-20\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Amazon Music Unlimited</a> or<a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/kindle-dbs/hz/subscribe/ku?tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"> Kindle Unlimited</a>, <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/fmc/learn-more?tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon Fresh</a>, plus several Amazon clothing brands, like&#160;<a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/fashion-sales-and-deals/b/?ie=UTF8&node=9538491011&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20-2020-20\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">GoodThreads and Daily Ritual</a>.</p><p>Prime members in the following countries can participate in the event: the US, UK, UAE, Spain, Singapore, Netherlands, Mexico, Luxembourg, Japan, Italy, Germany, France, China, Canada, Belgium, Austria, Australia, and — for the first time this year — Turkey and Brazil.</p><h3><strong>Was Amazon Prime Day postponed this year?</strong></h3><p>Prime Day in past years has always taken place during the summer, specifically in July. Due to recent supply-chain delays and increased demand related to the novel coronavirus pandemic, Amazon has pushed Prime Day 2020 to October 13-14.</p><h3><strong>Who can access Prime Day deals?</strong></h3><p>Only Amazon Prime members can take advantage of this event.&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-sign-up-for-prime\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"76cf80298ed4d10cbf1c26bafc19b794\">Signing up</a>&#160;is easy though, and a membership comes with&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazon-prime-benefits-what-is-included\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"0fbb4a7bd16726c880ad36bd78ad1161\">many more benefits</a>&#160;than just Prime Day deals access and free two-day shipping. New members can sign up for a&#160;<a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/tryprimefree?ots=1&slotNum=44&imprToken=26ba8e8c-b97a-0d2d-e64&ref_=assoc_tag_ph_1427739975520&_encoding=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=pf4&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=7c7ba50a8d1bc47669fb74f5edf22ea6kId=7c7ba50a8d1bc47669fb74f5edf22ea6\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"7911be800a637dc04838b84e8133bb3f\">free 30-day trial</a>&#160;with full benefits before committing.</p><p>We're currently in the sweet spot wherein you can sign up for the month-long&#160;<a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/tryprimefree?ots=1&slotNum=45&imprToken=26ba8e8c-b97a-0d2d-e64&ref_=assoc_tag_ph_1427739975520&_encoding=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=pf4&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=7c7ba50a8d1bc47669fb74f5edf22ea6kId=7c7ba50a8d1bc47669fb74f5edf22ea6\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"669f27d899857da1edf76666973c1ab7\">free trial</a>, shop&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-do-you-get-a-lightning-deal-on-amazon-prime-day\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"89068e83ef9b655558d8a95189078482\">Prime Day</a>, and avoid paying for the subscription cost. Of course, you can also just pay for a $13 month-long subscription to shop Prime Day, if you've already had a Prime subscription.</p><h3><strong>Do other stores take part in Amazon Prime Day?</strong></h3><p>Walmart, Target, and Best Buy will offer sales with competitive pricing during and around the event. However, the volume and quality of these competitor deals are up in the air, as the postponement of Prime Day 2020 has left us very close to Black Friday and Cyber Monday.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/walmart-prime-day-sale-deals\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"edfce1b550bcffc76218b1b38e73e593\">Walmart's \"Big Save Event\"</a>&#160;leapfrogged Prime Day by starting on October 11, and it will last until Thursday, October 15 – a day longer than Prime Day itself. However, it still remains to be seen how&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/walmart-plus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"2ba027311c1e8b3933e48ac9b99ad8e6\">Walmart+</a>, the retail giant's Amazon Prime \"competition,\" factors into the equation. It's likely that Walmart will have early offers and some exclusive discounts for subscribers. Fortunately,&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/walmart-plus-free-trial\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"a2703bfe9d375275a35c280128c44acc\">Walmart+ offers a 15-day free trial</a>.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/target-deal-days-prime-day-sale\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"9f2c82d470657e36716f7745b78f632f\">Target's 'Deal Days' event</a>&#160;matches Prime Day's dates and will offer shoppers \"double the deals compared to last year.\" As with Amazon Prime Day, Target will offer \"early-bird deals\" ahead of 'Deal Days' plus exclusive discounts for Target Circle members.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-buy-prime-day-deals-2020\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"b1db0d539f906c7f0cd8db0e9d875703\">Best Buy</a>&#160;has historically offered discounts during Prime Day and this year will be no different. During the sale, Best Buy will sell laptops starting as low as $120,&#160;<a href=\"https://bestbuy.7tiv.net/c/196318/614286/10014?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bestbuy.com%2Fsite%2Fjbl-free-true-wireless-in-ear-headphones-gen-2-white%2F6261395.p%3FskuId%3D6261395&subid2=1602511008047anatnnz6a&subId3=xid:fr1602511011458fjd11458fjd\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-orig-url=\"https://bestbuy.7tiv.net/c/196318/614286/10014?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bestbuy.com%2Fsite%2Fjbl-free-true-wireless-in-ear-headphones-gen-2-white%2F6261395.p%3FskuId%3D6261395&subid2=1602511008047anatnnz6anz6a\" data-ml-id=\"3\" data-ml=\"true\" data-xid=\"fr1602511011458fjd\" data-uri=\"1d6807e8d35e9221c0e2bfe14b77d4b9\">JBL Free true wireless headphones for $70</a>, and a Samsung 70-inch 4K smart TV for $530. Of course, Best Buy will reveal more as we get closer to the event. Shoppers, however, can expect to see discounts on Apple devices, laptops, big-screen TVs, and kitchen appliances during their competing Prime Day sale.</p><p>Best Buy, like Target and Walmart, price matches many of Amazon's discounts, with or without a formal event announcement. We'll be covering the best deals from these retailers, plus other notable stores and companies, during Prime Day, just as we do during the rest of the year.</p><h3><strong>How will this Prime Day be different from years past?</strong></h3><p>With Prime Day happening so close to Black Friday this year, competing sales and the number of overall deals will most likely be fewer in number.</p><p>Rival retailers may do as little as match Amazon's discounts on Amazon products, like&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazon-device-launch-2020\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"16e575f05c65752d3c4da66f84b5b446\">Kindles and Echo speakers</a>, and a few high-demand products, like Sony headphones or gaming consoles.&#160;</p><p>The larger ripple we expect to see this Amazon Prime Day is less available stock and potentially delayed shipping. Shipping speeds often take a hit during these high-traffic events, and we expect it to be worse than in years past.</p><p>With supply chains still not back up to snuff since prior to the pandemic, high-demand items like&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-webcam\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-uri=\"70fe57f75e514b31e92cb82b28409da4\">webcams</a>,&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/work-from-home-essentials-hub\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-uri=\"681886a0fe50e118e0281e3d973cad26\">home office furniture</a>, brand-name&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-hand-sanitizers\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-uri=\"a5ff5c8adfd8453d95b4d2a72bc8064b\">hand sanitizers</a>,&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-home-gym\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-uri=\"0e75c948d3edee2733efcf5907c33ba3\">workout equipment</a>,&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-sewing-machine\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-uri=\"4cf6fcb02377319a7f0f5f041c15522e\">sewing machines</a>, and the like will probably run out quickly, if they're in stock at all.</p><h3><strong>How do I prepare for Amazon Prime Day?</strong></h3><p>With Amazon Prime Day fast approaching, there are a few steps you can take to get the most out of the big shopping event. This prep can save you a ton of time and effort on the actual deal days and net you nearly $100 in account credit to use on October 13-14.</p><ol><li>Make sure you're an Amazon Prime member ahead of the sales event.</li><li>Download the Amazon app.</li><li>Shop Amazon's physical stores to collect bonus credit, refill your Amazon account balance, and apply for an Amazon.com Store card. Consider that just by shopping for groceries with Amazon, you can collect up to $50 in \"free money\" and adding an Amazon.com Store Card to your wallet will net you a $60 gift card.</li><li>Create a shopping plan and narrow down what you want to buy.&#160;</li></ol><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-shop-amazon-prime-day\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-uri=\"31099cc5832d92c7dec90bbf3bbc0c1a\">For more detailed information on how to get ready to shop Amazon Prime Day 2020, read this</a>.</p><p>You can also prepare by reading up on&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/category/prime-day-2020\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-uri=\"54b79bcf4c288232757a7795ae3b97c4\">everything Prime Day-related</a>&#160;to learn about what types of deals to expect and how to shop special promotions like Lightning Deals.&#160;</p><p>We recommend holding off on buying Amazon devices and services until deals start to go live, if you can. While we also expect other smart home brands to drop in price considerably, brands like Kindle and Echo are our for-sure bet to drop in price. We also recommend waiting to sign up for any Amazon services or memberships, like&#160;<a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/dmusic/promotions/AmazonMusicUnlimitedref_=assoc_tag_ph_1483579440886&_encoding=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=pf4&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=7c1e59d11f5ad56ec72254ff223bbd5d?ots=1&slotNum=46&imprToken=26ba8e8c-b97a-0d2d-e64imprToken=26ba8e8c-b97a-0d2d-e64\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-amzn-asin=\"promotions\" data-uri=\"f1b722e87c8e880ee47a1d1290ca987d\">Amazon Music Unlimited</a>&#160;or&#160;<a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/kindle-dbs/hz/signup?ots=1&slotNum=47&imprToken=26ba8e8c-b97a-0d2d-e64&ref_=assoc_tag_ph_1454291293420&_encoding=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=pf4&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=213203c0cd7efa1c6516de594c313a7fkId=213203c0cd7efa1c6516de594c313a7f\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-uri=\"a8ee976b4e6b5ddfdedc6da54541c646\">Kindle Unlimited</a>, as they often drop down to record-breaking lows during Prime Day.</p><p>If one of the products on your wish list didn't receive a discount during Prime Day — don't immediately surrender to the retail price. In a little more than a month after Prime Day, Black Friday and Cyber Monday may offer the discount you were hoping for.</p><h3><strong style=\"color: #000000;\">Which is better for deals: Prime Day or Black Friday?</strong></h3><p>2020 has been an unprecedented year for deals events, so making solid predictions based on past years is somewhat difficult. However, we can expect Amazon-branded merchandise (e.g.,&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazon-device-launch-2020\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-uri=\"16e575f05c65752d3c4da66f84b5b446\">Kindle, Echo, Ring, etc.</a>) to be at all-time lows during Prime Day, the company's own event.&#160;</p><p>We could speculate for days whether or not retailers will be able to offer equally jaw-dropping prices as past years, but with the delays in supply chains and shipping, and demand increases, prices this year between either Prime Day or Black Friday may not be as great as in past years (if there's even enough stock).</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Courtesy of Walmart</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>We often highlight stories of digital overhauls that enable <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/bed-bath-and-beyond-google-cloud-2020-9\">faster business growth</a>, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/phillips-66-sap-it-modernization-cloud-digital-transformation-2020-7\">deeper operational cost cuts</a>, and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-this-secretive-ai-startup-is-helping-call-center-employees-2020-4\">more seamless interactions with customers</a>.&#160;</p><p>But there's another component to transformations, too: reputation.&#160;</p><p>Walmart, for example, is <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/walmart-perfects-employee-feedback-loop-on-artificial-intelligence-2019-8\">investing heavily in technology,</a> both as part of its epic battle with Amazon for retail dominance and from a <a href=\"https://www.cnbc.com/2019/03/10/at-sxsw-this-year-walmart-bills-itself-as-a-tech-company.html\">desire to be viewed as a software behemoth</a>. The company <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/the-ai-partners-walmart-working-with-become-a-software-giant-2020-7\">works with a slew of outside vendors</a>, but is developing <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/walmart-ai-leader-uses-3-questions-to-guide-its-efforts-2019-10\">many of applications in-house, as well</a> — like its <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/walmart-rolls-out-express-delivery-brings-orders-under-two-hours-2020-5\">recent express delivery option</a>. The overhaul is so robust that some Wall Street analysts believe Walmart's stock should be treated more like that of a tech company.</p><p>In the case of Aventiv Technologies — the parent-firm of prison communications company Securus Technologies that's backed by billionaire Tom Gores — new CEO Dave Abel is <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/securus-dave-abel-tom-gores-digital-aventiv-prison-controversial-image-2020-9\">relying on a digital overhaul to rebuild a tattered public image</a>.&#160;</p><p>Securus has faced heavy criticism over the past few years for the costs it charges prison inmates to use the services, which lawsuits allege is sometimes as high as $15.99 for a 15-minute call. But Abel is promising sweeping changes and&#160;Securus poured an additional $30 million into its tech budget —&#160;on top of the $50 million it already spends annually.&#160;</p><p>\"We believe that the incarcerated community is worthy of the investment of capital. We believe they're worthy of technology,\" Abel told me. \"Part of our transformation has been convincing and demonstrating to the leadership of our company and within our company that digital transformation has the opportunity for us to refocus personnel in the organization to create greater value.\"&#160;</p><p>Abel says the company reduced the average call cost to 15 cents a minute, a 30% cut from earlier rates, and it provided 26 million free calls during the coronavirus pandemic. But that hasn't stopped some customers from <a href=\"https://www.adn.com/alaska-news/crime-courts/2020/09/20/facing-an-indefinite-ban-on-in-person-visits-families-of-alaska-prisoners-question-paid-phone-calls/\">spending hundreds of dollars a month to talk to family members</a>.</p><p>Below are a few other stories that you may have missed from the last two weeks. border=\"0\"></img></a>\n</div><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/PsK1nZ3tNTQ\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" alt=\"\"/>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Mon, 12 Oct 2020 16:22:18 +0000","feedId":22,"bgimg":"https://i.insider.com/5f847c05bab422001979ac89?format=jpeg","linkMd5":"a1deda2bf2c93590a213e9e1d12efecb","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn20@2020_4/2020/10/12/17-04-54-151_0fe558950606d698.webp","destWidth":1781,"destHeight":1336,"sourceBytes":123244,"destBytes":123244,"author":"jwilliams@businessinsider.com (Joe Williams)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/5e2b1d1762fa8128e4415854?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn70@2020_3/2020/10/12/17-04-52-652_791ec2834b945d54.webp","https://i.insider.com/5f847bf7642e9400180b559f?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn99@2020_4/2020/10/12/17-04-59-997_7b0a174eda1c784d.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn28@2020_6/2020/10/12/17-05-01-063_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=PsK1nZ3tNTQ:FYSokDrUUPU:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn88@2020_5/2020/10/12/17-04-59-026_5eac39e1bdb03631.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=PsK1nZ3tNTQ:FYSokDrUUPU:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn43@2020_2/2020/10/12/17-04-59-653_f8caf06504dce46c.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn68@2020_5/2020/10/12/17-04-57-018_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=PsK1nZ3tNTQ:FYSokDrUUPU:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn15@2020_6/2020/10/12/17-05-00-089_876fc43abed54667.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/PsK1nZ3tNTQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn16@2020_4/2020/10/12/17-04-55-057_0a1dc6e873f57e62.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1602522289793},{"createdTime":"2020-10-13 01:04:49","updatedTime":"2020-10-13 01:04:49","title":"Former Marvel execs launched an ambitious comics universe as the pandemic hit. 7 months later, they have Hollywood in their sights.","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/former-marvel-execs-new-comics-company-awa-business-interview-2020-10","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f7f69c94c3b2e0019bb9fae?format=jpeg\" alt=\"AWA comics\" height=\"1228\" width=\"1772\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>AWA previewed its comics at last year&#39;s New York Comic Con.\n<p class=\"copyright\">AWA</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Two former Marvel executives, Axel Alonso and Bill Jemas, along with Fandom cochairman Jon Miller, founded the new comics company Artists, Writers and Artisans (AWA) last year.</li>\n<li>The company launched its first comic series, \"The Resistance,\" in March, shortly before comics distribution was halted due to the pandemic.</li>\n<li>Business Insider talked with Alonso and Jemas about navigating a new comic publisher through the pandemic, how it's performing, and what to expect from its future.&#160;</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Two former Marvel execs, Axel Alonso and Bill Jemas, entered 2020 expecting to go full steam ahead with a new comics universe. Not only did they have decades of combined experience in the industry, but also financial backing from big-time investors like James Murdoch, the son of media mogul Rupert Murdoch.</p><p>But it didn't take long before they hit a complication. Their new company, Artists, Writers and Artisans (AWA), debuted its first series in March. Five days after it was released, comics distribution was halted and shops across the country closed due to the pandemic.</p><p>That first series, AWA's \"The Resistance,\" by writer J. Michael Straczynski and artist Mike Deodato Jr., was coincidentally about a virus that kills millions around the world, but gives thousands of others superpowers. It is meant to set up AWA's \"shared universe,\" similar to Marvel and DC's in which characters live in the same universe and can interact with one another.</p><p>The distribution shutdown was painful for AWA.</p><p>\"Knowing that 'The Resistance' was sitting on the racks in the comic shops and people couldn't get it was a nightmare,\" Alonso said.</p><p>But he wouldn't call the pandemic a setback for the company.</p><p>While comics distribution was shut down, AWA released \"The Resistance\" as a free digital comic, boosting awareness for the series for when the comics shutdown ended in May and readers returned to stores.&#160;</p><p>\"You have to look where there's an opportunity to be discovered in a crisis,\" Alonso said. \"People liked it, so when shops opened back up, they flew off the shelves. Comic readers are completionists. Just because they read it online doesn't deter them to buy the comic or graphic novel.\"</p><p>Alonso has experience seeing opportunity in crisis, having started AWA after exiting his position as Marvel's editor-in-chief during a 2017 sales slump.&#160;</p><p>He also has faith that AWA's vision of a new business model for comics, where risk and upside are split between the creator and publisher, will be able to entice creators to build a comics universe to compete with heavyweights Marvel and DC.</p><h2>Alonso's Marvel exit was the catalyst for AWA</h2><p>Alonso is well aware of the irony in that AWA's first series was about a pandemic, but that aligns with one of his missions for the company: reflecting the real world, which was born out of his experience at Marvel.</p><p>Alonso was editor-in-chief starting in 2011, during a time <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/marvel-insiders-describe-lack-diversity-editorial-leadership-2020-7\">when Marvel introduced bold and diverse new characters</a> like Miles Morales, a biracial Spider-Man. But when sales had decreased in 2017, Alonso was ousted.</p><p>\"One of my goals was to introduce more diversity,\" Alonso said of Marvel. \"It deeply offended some long-term fans. But to see Miles Morales on the big screen [in \"Spider-Man: Into the Spider-Verse\"] was validating. It showed that being topical was a good thing. It's a foolish path to make the fans love you. Now I start the day looking at a blank canvas. You have to take chances, go with your gut, and write about the world as it is.&#160;</p><p>He was contemplating his next move in late 2018 when he got a call from Jemas, another comics veteran.</p><p>Jemas, the former president of Marvel Comics who is often credited for helping dig the company out of bankruptcy in the early 2000s, was exploring a new venture, and he wanted Alonso at his side. Jemas had previously poached Alonso for Marvel from DC in 2000.</p><p>Jemas called Alonso's departure from Marvel the spark for AWA.</p><p>\"Axel is the best there is at what he does,\" Jemas told Business Insider.</p><p>These two former Marvel execs, along with Jon Miller, the cochairman of entertainment website Fandom, joined forces for a comics company at the intersection of titanic publishers like Marvel and DC and creator-owned publishers like Image. Jemas serves as CEO, Alonso as creative chief, and Miller as board chairman.</p><p>\"In comics, you can either go to Marvel or DC and get a page rate but own nothing, or option B is creator-owned,\" Alonso said. \"You can do something original that you own and put out in the market and hope it finds an audience. If you're lucky and your book becomes the next 'Walking Dead,' you have a stable income. If not, you may not make much money.\"</p><p>AWA aims to mitigate the risks for creators when launching a creator-owned comic by guaranteeing them a financial stake in the books. At Marvel or DC, creators take on little risk but own none of the IP. At a publisher like Image, they own their IP, but take on most of the financial risk. AWA aims to split the risk between the creator and the publisher.</p><p>\"We do budget each series to be cash-flow positive, but our publishing business doesn't cover our overhead costs,\" Jemas said. \"We don't expect it to until we build up a solid backlist of graphic novels and hardcover books.\"</p><p>Jemas said that sales have been above projections. \"The Resistance\" issue one landed at No. 65 on industry website Comichron's best-selling comics of March, a list dominated by much larger publishers Marvel and DC, with more than 26,000 copies sold.&#160;</p><p>Alonso said AWA's model allows creators to \"bet on themselves without putting it all on the line.\"</p><p>That's what attracted AWA's \"Year Zero\" and \"Devil's Highway\" writer Benjamin Percy to AWA. Known for DC comics like \"Green Arrow\" and currently Marvel's \"Wolverine,\" Percy got to experiment with AWA.</p><p>\"Writing for DC and Marvel is a privilege and a joy of course, but it also comes with restrictions, because you're often the custodian of a character that's been around for decades,\" Percy told Business Insider.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f7f6c3aea74820019ca608a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"AWA\" height=\"1164\" width=\"1742\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A group of AWA characters.\n<p class=\"copyright\">AWA/Mike Deodato Jr</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><h2>Hollywood is in AWA's sights</h2><p>At a time when Hollywood is increasingly looking for new IP to mine, AWA's mission attracted major investors.</p><p>They include production company Sister, which was founded by Elisabeth Murdoch (the daughter of Rupert), and Stacey Snider, the former chair and CEO of Fox's film studio; James Murdoch, the son of Rupert, who has distanced himself from his father's media empire that includes Fox News and News Corp; and the venture capital firm Lightspeed Venture Partners.&#160;</p><p>\"There's an arms race for great content right now between Netflix, Amazon, Hulu and Disney itself, with Disney Plus,\" Alex Taussig, a partner at Lightspeed Venture Partners, told <a href=\"https://www.wsj.com/articles/james-murdoch-is-investing-his-fortune-one-bet-comic-books-11555424725\">The Wall Street Journal</a> last year.</p><p>Both Sister and James Murdoch invested at least $5 million into the company, according to WSJ. Miller, the third AWA founder who is also a former digital chief at News Corp, facilitated Murdoch's investment, WSJ said.&#160;</p><p>\"[James] Murdoch knows comic books and respected our vision,\" Alonso said. \"He loved that we were empowering creators and giving them skin in the game. He liked that creators would be invested in it and he saw potential in that.\"</p><p>The goal is to eventually make the move to Hollywood and discussions have taken place, Jemas and Percy said, but they didn't disclose further details.</p><p>\"Hollywood is hungry for IP,\" Percy said. \"One of the questions you always face with studios is the question, 'What does it look like?' You show them a comic and the whole project is already storyboarded.\"</p><p>The comics will always come first, Alonso said.&#160;</p><p>\"Our goal is to create a respected publisher first,\" he said. \"We have to make comic books first. I'm not a director or screenwriter or showrunner. I make comic books. But I want to make comic books that people would want to see on the screen.\"</p><p>But Alonso also noted, \"No one does comics saying 'I hope we just end here.'\" Once the comics universe has strong enough legs, it's inevitable that AWA will try to make the leap to movies and TV.</p><p>The future plans for those comics?</p><p>Alonso said that the second volume of \"The Resistance\" has already been written and is being drawn. He compared the books to TV seasons, meaning they'll be told in different volumes but will be an ongoing story. Readers can expect work from popular creators like Reginald Hudlin, Garth Ennis, and Frank Cho, who are all on the company's creative council.&#160;</p><p>\"The number one rule when we spoke to investors and amongst ourselves is to be patient,\" Alonso said.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a 01:04:49","updatedTime":"2020-10-13 01:04:49","title":"Gov. Andrew Cuomo says he has 'no interest in going to Washington' amid rumors of Attorney General post under a Biden administration","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/andrew-cuomo-governor-new-york-attorney-general-joe-biden-2020-10","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f8460f7642e9400180b5505?format=jpeg\" alt=\"cuomo\" height=\"2057\" width=\"2742\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Governor Andrew Cuomo (D-New York) speaks at a press conference.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Lev Radin/Pacific Press/LightRocket via Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Gov. Andrew Cuomo of New York on Monday dismissed rumors that he was being considered as US Attorney General in a possible Biden administration.</li>\n<li>The Cabinet speculation was ignited by <a href=\"https://www.axios.com/andrew-cuomo-biden-attorney-general-97fba9a0-03c5-4709-80b9-5e254c2e1e1f.html\">an Axios report</a> that was published over the weekend.</li>\n<li>Cuomo said that he \"had no interest in going to Washington,\" adding that \"those rumors are only from people who want to get me out of New York.\"</li>\n<li>From 1997 to 2001, Cuomo served as the Secretary of Housing and Urban Development under then-President Bill Clinton.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>New York Gov. Andrew Cuomo on Monday shot down any speculation that he would be interested in becoming the US Attorney General under a potential Biden administration, following <a href=\"https://www.axios.com/andrew-cuomo-biden-attorney-general-97fba9a0-03c5-4709-80b9-5e254c2e1e1f.html\">an Axios report released</a> over the weekend.</p><p>When asked about the report on NBC's \"Today\" show, Cuomo said that he had \"no interest in going to Washington\" despite his longtime friendship with Democratic presidential nominee Joe Biden. He also relayed how he would respond to the former vice president if the position was offered to him.</p><p>\"I would say, 'You are an old friend. You are a good friend. You're going to win this election. You're going to be the president. I'll help you any way I can,'\" Cuomo said.</p><p>\"I'm a New Yorker. I said I would serve as governor,\" he added. \"And those rumors are only from people who want to get me out of New York. I don't know why, but that's where that's coming from ... I said when this COVID situation started, just so I had total credibility with the people of the state, 'I'm not running for president. I'm not running for vice president. I don't want to go to Washington.'\"</p><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet blockquote\" data-lang=\"en\" data-cards=\"\" data-conversation=\"\">&#8212;TODAY  (@TODAYshow) <a href=\"https://twitter.com/mims/statuses/1315631409495769092?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\">October 12, 2020</a></blockquote><script async src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><p><a href=\"https://www.axios.com/andrew-cuomo-biden-attorney-general-97fba9a0-03c5-4709-80b9-5e254c2e1e1f.html\">The Axios article</a> stated that the Attorney General role \"would be among the most politically sensitive and high-profile jobs in a Biden administration\" and that \"the Justice Department will face pressure to investigate Trump-era officials — and perhaps Trump himself — for wrongdoing in office.\"</p><p>Cuomo has served as governor of New York since 2011 and was easily reelected to his second and third terms, in 2014 and 2018, respectively. In May 2019, <a href=\"https://www.governing.com/topics/politics/tns-cuomo-will-run-for-governor-2022.html\">he told Governing magazine</a> that he was planning to run for a fourth term as governor in 2022. Unlike most states, New York does not have term limits for governors.</p><p>Before he served as the state's chief executive, Cuomo was New York's attorney general from 2007 to 2011. And he is no stranger to Washington, having served as Secretary of Housing and Urban Development under then-President Bill Clinton from 1997 to 2001.&#160;</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/andrew-cuomo-governor-new-york-attorney-general-joe-biden-2020-10'>Business Insider</a></div><div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?a=JQ4IBpmg4rE:VnFUThubak0:yIl2AUoC8zA\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA\" border=\"0\"></img></a> <a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?a=JQ4IBpmg4rE:VnFUThubak0:F7zBnMyn0Lo\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=JQ4IBpmg4rE:VnFUThubak0:F7zBnMyn0Lo\" border=\"0\"></img></a> <a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?a=JQ4IBpmg4rE:VnFUThubak0:V_sGLiPBpWU\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=JQ4IBpmg4rE:VnFUThubak0:V_sGLiPBpWU\" border=\"0\"></img></a> <a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?a=JQ4IBpmg4rE:VnFUThubak0:qj6IDK7rITs\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs\" border=\"0\"></img></a> <a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?a=JQ4IBpmg4rE:VnFUThubak0:gIN9vFwOqvQ\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=JQ4IBpmg4rE:VnFUThubak0:gIN9vFwOqvQ\" border=\"0\"></img></a>\n</div><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/JQ4IBpmg4rE\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" alt=\"\"/>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Mon, 12 Oct 2020 15:55:10 +0000","feedId":22,"bgimg":"https://i.insider.com/5f846123642e9400180b5506?format=jpeg","linkMd5":"66b9b20f53688802b21d280a6a846b0a","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn82@2020_6/2020/10/12/17-04-54-020_ed69f34e016eaf94.webp","destWidth":2742,"destHeight":2057,"sourceBytes":172136,"destBytes":172136,"author":"insider@insider.com (John L. Dorman)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/5f8460f7642e9400180b5505?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn40@2020_3/2020/10/12/17-04-56-033_5b1149e03f4cb44d.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn28@2020_6/2020/10/12/17-05-01-063_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=JQ4IBpmg4rE:VnFUThubak0:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn9@2020_3/2020/10/12/17-05-03-488_6ed5af2dee6618eb.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=JQ4IBpmg4rE:VnFUThubak0:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn76@2020_3/2020/10/12/17-04-59-885_2c2aa112413c3460.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn68@2020_5/2020/10/12/17-04-57-018_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=JQ4IBpmg4rE:VnFUThubak0:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn91@2020_5/2020/10/12/17-05-00-035_2ca67705c140b4c5.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/JQ4IBpmg4rE":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn24@2020_4/2020/10/12/17-05-01-905_a00760c16d775b4a.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1602522289822},{"createdTime":"2020-10-13 01:04:49","updatedTime":"2020-10-13 01:04:49","title":"Before the AC-130, the Air Force had another fearsome gunship","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/before-the-ac130-the-air-force-had-another-fearsome-gunship-2020-10","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f83e78f642e9400180b5475?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Douglas AC-47D\" height=\"897\" width=\"1795\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A US Air Force Douglas AC-47D in South Vietnam in September 1968.\n<p class=\"copyright\">US Air Force</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>The AC-130s has been the Air Force's gunship for decades.</li>\n<li>But before the AC-130, another fearsome gunship poured fire onto targets to support troops on the ground.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>The C-47 fulfilled a number of roles in World War II and Korea. It was a supply plane, a plane for dropping paratroopers, and a tow for gliders.</p><p>But it was in the Vietnam War that the \"<a href=\"http://www.boeing.com/history/products/c-47-skytrain.page\">Gooney Bird</a>\" would get its greatest mission — flying three 7.62 mm miniguns through the night to devastate North Vietnamese and Viet Cong forces.</p><p>The idea for a side-firing gunship had been <a href=\"https://books.google.com/books?id=FW_50wm8VnMC&pg=PA284&lpg=PA284&dq=DH-4+side+mounted+machine+gun&source=bl&ots=ShhNw4zhZL&sig=GfVH189dd2J-FQ3iJJyYsxNKVz0&hl=en&sa=X&ved=0ahUKEwiYw9j80e_RAhXBPCYKHVqODfAQ6AEIQzAL#v=onepage&q=DH-4%20side%20mounted%20machine%20gun&f=false20side%20mounted%20machine%20gun&#38;f=false\">floating around military circles since at least 1926</a>. In fact, the technique had been tested successfully in 1927 when 1st Lt. Fred Nelson flew a DH-4 with a mounted .30-cal machine gun and destroyed a target on the ground.</p><p>But the Army Air Corps and the Army Air Forces never came around to the idea. It was 1963 before the idea of a side-firing aircraft got another serious test. A C-131B modified with gunsights and a minigun was successful in early tests and the experiment was repeated with a C-47.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f83e7b3bab422001979ab67?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Douglas AC-47D MXU-470 miniguns\" height=\"768\" width=\"1024\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The three MXU-470/A minigun modules fitted to an AC-47D.\n<p class=\"copyright\">US Air Force</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>The C-47 performed swimmingly as well, and Air Force leader <a href=\"http://www.historynet.com/spooky-gunship-operations-in-the-vietnam-war.htm\">Gen. Curtis LeMay approved the modification of two planes in 1964</a>.</p><p>The final combat variant of the AC-47 consisted of the cargo plane with three 7.62 mm miniguns mounted on the left side — two in modified portholes near the cargo door and one in the cargo door itself. The triggers for the three guns were connected to a button in the pilot's compartment.</p><p>The pilots would take off with a <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=-ojAAEgVJ84\">seven-man crew</a> and seek out small bases and villages under fire by North Vietnamese forces. When fighting popped off, <a href=\"https://books.google.com/books?id=RfRvCwAAQBAJ&pg=PT285&lpg=PT285&dq=AC-47+korea&source=bl&ots=7oxU-PAyi5&sig=lN0d_Ca2ObLoebpBaGIMHiS3DlE&hl=en&sa=X&ved=0ahUKEwj1lJ3mu-_RAhUO3iYKHR94DzgQ6AEIWDAL#v=onepage&q=AC-47%20korea&f=falseAL#v=onepage&#38;q=AC-47%20korea&#38;f=false\">the crew would drop flares out of the open door and the pilot would fly a race track pattern over the target</a>, pouring fire on it the whole time.</p><p>If the threat was too large for the AC-47, the flares it dropped would light up the target for follow-on fighters. The AC-47 would stay in the area, directing the attacks by other aircraft.</p><p>The AC-47, dubbed \"Puff, the Magic Dragon,\" by an officer who saw it at work, was so effective that the Air Force launched Project Gunship II, the program which resulted in the AC-130 still in service today.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5420343becad044f32be14cb?format=jpeg\" alt=\"AC 130H Spectre\" height=\"2036\" width=\"3066\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>An AC-130H Spectre gunship.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Senior Airman Julianne Showalter/USAF</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>A number of AC-47 pilots and crew members were cited for bravery while serving aboard the plane, including <a href=\"http://valor.militarytimes.com/recipient.php?recipientid=1957\">Medal of Honor recipient Sgt. John L. Levitow</a>. Levitow was on an AC-47 that was struck by a mortar round.</p><p>Though he was peppered by approximately 40 pieces of shrapnel in the blast, he noticed that a flare — activated by another crewmember just before the blast — was rolling around the cargo area.</p><p>The flare had yet to fully ignite, but it was only a matter of time before it would, possibly killing the crew on its own and almost certainly causing the cargo hold of ammunition to go off.</p><p>Levitow crawled to the flare, held the burning implement against his already wounded body, and moved to the door with it. He was able to throw it out just before the flare ignited.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/before-the-ac130-the-air-force-had-another-fearsome-gunship-2020-10'>Business Insider</a></div><div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>YouTube CEO Susan Wojcicki isn't committing to an outright ban of QAnon content on the platform.&#160;</li>\n<li>Wojcicki was asked about banning QAnon, a baseless far-right conspiracy theory, during <a href=\"https://www.cnn.com/2020/10/12/tech/youtube-susan-wojcicki-boss-files/index.html\">an interview with CNN's Poppy href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Facebook may have <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/qanon-banned-from-facebook-dealing-massive-blow-to-conspiracy-group-2020-10\">banned QAnon content from all of its platforms</a>, but Susan Wojcicki isn't committing to doing the same on YouTube.</p><p>The YouTube CEO on Monday <a href=\"https://www.cnn.com/2020/10/12/tech/youtube-susan-wojcicki-boss-files/index.html\">told CNN's Poppy Harlow</a> that the company is looking \"very closely\" at videos relating to the conspiracy-theory movement QAnon, but wouldn't say whether YouTube has plans to institute an outright ban, citing the movement's leaderless nature as a factor.&#160;</p><p>\"I think if you look at QAnon, part of it is that it's a grassroots movement, and so you could see just lots and lots of different people who are uploading content that has different QAnon theories,\" Wojcicki said. \"We're very proactive in terms of removing it, and I think you'll see us continue to be so.\"&#160;</p><p>Wojcicki said YouTube has implemented multiple policies to curb the spread of QAnon content, including making changes to its recommendations tool, which she said have resulted in an 80% reduction in views on QAnon videos. In addition, YouTube has already removed \"hundreds of thousands\" of QAnon videos for violating other parts of the platform's policies, like those prohibiting COVID-19 misinformation or hate and harassment, Wojcicki said.</p><p>\"I would say we already implemented a large number of different policies that have helped to maintain that in a responsible way,\" Wojcicki said, adding that YouTube's policies are continuing to evolve. \"It's not that we're not looking at it,\" she said.</p><p>QAnon is a baseless far-right conspiracy theory that claims President Donald Trump is secretly fighting a \"deep state\" cabal of satanic pedophiles and cannibals. The FBI has labeled QAnon a domestic-terrorism threat.</p><p>QAnon emerged on online message boards like 4Chan in 2017 before moving to mainstream social media sites like Facebook and YouTube, as <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/youtube-still-hosts-qanon-despite-facebook-crackdown-2020-10\">Business Insider's Tom Porter pointed out</a>. YouTube has since become rife with videos promoting the conspiracy theory. Last month, <a href=\"https://www.journalism.org/2020/09/28/many-americans-get-news-on-youtube-where-news-organizations-and-independent-producers-thrive-side-by-side/\">a study from Pew Research Center</a> found that QAnon is the most commonly mentioned conspiracy theory among the most-viewed independent news channels on the platform.&#160;</p><p>When Facebook <a href=\"https://about.fb.com/news/2020/08/addressing-movements-and-organizations-tied-to-violence/\">announced its QAnon ban</a> earlier this month, it said that it wouldn't remove individual posts pertaining to the conspiracy theory, only Facebook Pages and Groups, and Instagram accounts representing QAnon. Wojcicki told CNN that YouTube is \"very different\" from Facebook and would need to first define a clear policy around what QAnon is.&#160;</p><p>\"I think the way to approach it is by actually having the policies implemented in the right way,\" she said. \"And our platform is very different from how Facebook works. And so I think each of us will take an approach that makes the most sense for our platforms.\"</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f8457d2642e9400180b54de?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Amy Coney Barrett.JPG\" height=\"1000\" width=\"2000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>U.S. Supreme Court nominee Judge Amy Coney REUTERS</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>The Senate Judiciary Committee began confirmation hearings Monday morning to confirm Judge Amy Coney Barrett to the Supreme href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>The Senate Judiciary Committee began confirmation hearings Monday morning to confirm Judge Amy Coney Barrett. The hearings kick off an accelerated process to confirm Barrett before the November 3 presidential election.&#160;</p><p>Barrett was nominated by President Donald Trump to fill the seat vacated by Justice Ruth Bader Ginsburg, who died on September 18 at the age of 87 from pancreatic cancer.&#160;</p><p>After opening statements, Barrett will undergo two long long days of questioning on her judicial record and philosophy before the committee goes to a vote.&#160;</p><h2>Who is Amy Coney Barrett?</h2><p>Barrett, a favored pick of social conservatives, was nominated and confirmed to serve as a federal judge on the 7th Circuit Court of Appeals in Chicago in 2017.</p><p>Previously, she served for fifteen years as a law professor teaching constitutional law, statutory interpretation, and the federal courts at the University of Notre Dame, where she was lauded for her scholarship and beloved by students.&#160;</p><p>A star student in law school, Coney Barrett served in clerkships for Judge Laurence Silberman of the US Court of Appeals for the District of Columbia Circuit and for former Associate Justice Antonin Scalia of the US Supreme Court, who she now identifies as her top mentor.</p><p>Coney Barrett was one of Scalia's favorite clerks, and largely embodies his judicial philosophy of textualism, <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/2020/09/20/us/politics/supreme-court-barrett.html\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"60\" data-uri=\"4c7e5d2677b2d24861e7a7f2a00b5308\">The New York Times reported.&#160;</a></p><p>At age 48, Coney Barrett could serve decades on the court if confirmed. She is also the mother of seven children and would be the first mother of school-aged children to serve on the high court.&#160;</p><h2>How long will hearings run?&#160;</h2><p>Senate Judiciary Chairman Sen. Lindsey Graham said that the first day of the hearings will consist of opening statements, in which every member and Barrett herself will have ten minutes to speak.</p><p>The first day of statements is set to wrap up Monday afternoon. On Tuesday and Wednesday, Barrett will undergo two intense days of questioning from members about her judicial philosophy, her record on the bench so far, and how she might rule on future cases — especially those related to healthcare.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/amy-coney-barrett-hearings-supreme-court/2020/10/11/182255b4-0bbe-11eb-8a35-237ef1eb2ef7_story.html\">The Washington Post reported on Sunday</a> that Democrats are expected to put a narrow, laser-focus on Barrett's position on the Affordable Care Act, the landmark 2009 healthcare legislation that is currently being challenged in court by Republicans.&#160;</p><p>On Thursday, the Committee will hear from a number of outside witnesses and legal experts testifying in favor of and against Barrett's confirmation to the Court.&#160;</p><p>After four days of hearings, Graham said, the Judiciary Committee will go to markup to vote on advancing her confirmation to the Senate floor on October 22.&#160;</p><h2>Where can I watch the hearings?&#160;</h2><p>The hearings are being broadcast on every major cable news network <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=BrkD9mfvrB8\">and on C-SPAN</a>.&#160;</p><p>If you don't have a cable login, multiple news organizations and C-SPAN are live-streaming the hearings for free <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/results?search_query=amy+coney+barrett\">on YouTube</a> or <a href=\"https://www.npr.org/sections/live-amy-coney-barrett-supreme-court-confirmation/2020/10/12/921392600/watch-live-amy-coney-barretts-supreme-court-confirmation-hearing\">on their websites.</a></p><p>You can also watch the hearings on the Apple TV, Roku, Google Play, Android, iOS, and Amazon apps for cable news outlets like CNN, MSNBC, and Fox.&#160;</p><div Epstein regularly invited Black to his mansion in New York for breakfast or lunch, they said.</p><p>A spokesperson for Black confirmed that between 2012 and 2017 he had received \"personal trusts and estates planning advice as well as family office philanthropy and investment services from several financial and legal advisors,\" including Epstein.</p><p>Epstein, who was an American financier, was convicted for soliciting prostitution from a teenage girl in 2008 and served 13 months in a state jail. He was arrested again in July 2019, on federal charges for the sex trafficking of minors, and died in his jail cell in August 2019. His death was ruled a suicide.</p><h3>Payment drew scrutiny at Deutsche Bank</h3><p>According to documents reviewed by the Times, a company called BV70 LLC, which owned Black's yacht, made a $22.5 million payment in 2017 to Plan D, a firm that managed Epstein's Gulfstream jet.</p><p>The payment drew scrutiny at Deutsche Bank, where Epstein kept his accounts, according to a report from the bank reviewed by the paper. The report showed that the money was for consulting services for an entity Epstein operated in the Virgin Islands, the paper said.</p><p>BV70 also made a $10 million donation in 2015 to Gratitude America, an Epstein charitable foundation. The Deutsche Bank report showed that the company planned to make another $10 million payment to Epstein for advisory work, but it is unclear if the payment was ever made, the paper reported.</p><p>Stephanie Pillersdorf, a spokeswoman for Black, confirmed he had received advice from Epstein between 2012 and 2017. The advice was vetted by leading auditors and law firms, she said.</p><p>Black stopped business and communication with Epstein in 2018 following a \"fee dispute,\" Pillersdorf said.</p><p>Apollo never carried out any business with Epstein, she said.</p><p style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Black \"continues to be appalled by the conduct that led to the criminal charges\" against Epstein, she said, adding that Black \"deeply regrets having any involvement\" with Epstein.&#160;</p><p>Business Insider reported in July 2019 that <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/jeffrey-epstein-was-director-of-leon-blacks-foundation-for-10-years-2019-7\">Epstein was listed as the director</a> of the Leon Black Family Foundation from 2001 to 2012, according to tax filings. However, the foundation issued a statement the next day claiming that <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/leon-blacks-foundation-says-epstein-resigned-2019-7\">the tax returns were filed in error</a> and that Epstein had actually resigned in 2007.</p><p style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Black isn't the only Wall Street billionaire connected to Epstein. In December 2019, Celina Dubin, the daughter of billionaire hedge-fund manager Glenn Dubin and the former Miss Sweden Eva Andersson Dubin, was named as <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/investigation-of-jeffrey-epsteins-finances-reveals-trust-and-payments-2019-12\">one of the beneficiaries of a trust</a> Epstein also used to pay lawyers, models, and other associates in his circle, according to financial records.</p><p>A spokesperson for the Dubin family said at the time that Celina, who was 24 years old, didn't know anything about the trust, and there was no evidence that Epstein had a romantic relationship with her.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a The retailer decided to have it early this year \"to help shoppers start their shopping season early — and safely.\"</p><p>Best Buy promises that customers will have \"more ways to shop safely than ever before, including contactless curbside pickup\" plus new safety guidelines in-store.&#160;</p><bi-shortcode id=\"table-of-contents-sticky\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-type=\"h2\">Table of Contents: Masthead Sticky</bi-shortcode><h2>What deals should I expect?</h2><p>While Best Buy has yet to reveal all the discounts for the event, it highlighted a few upcoming deals. Shoppers can expect heavy discounts on products from Best Buy's in-house brands, including Insignia, Rocketfish, Dynex, and Init.</p><p>Best Buy will also likely match many of the discounts offered by <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazon-prime-day-best-deals\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Amazon</a>, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/target-deal-days-prime-day-sale\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Target</a>, and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/walmart-prime-day-sale-deals\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Walmart</a> on top brands like Samsung, Apple, Microsoft, and more.&#160;</p><h2>The best early Best Buy deals</h2><div id=\"ProductCard_5ec53728988ee33fe25d3829\" style=\"position:relative; top:0; left: 0\"></iframe></div><h2>When is Best Buy's competing Prime Day sale?&#160;</h2><p>Best Buy, like Amazon, will offer massive discounts on October 13 and 14. Historically, Best Buy's Black Friday sales event occurs directly after Thanksgiving Day, so this sale is much earlier than usual.</p><p>Earlier this year, Best Buy announced that it <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/retailers-closing-their-doors-on-thanksgiving-full-list-2020-7\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">would be one of several companies that would close stores during Thanksgiving</a> and claimed that it would offer holiday deals earlier to accommodate for its closure.&#160;</p><p>Of course, it remains to be seen whether the deals we see on October 13 and 14 will represent the entirety of Best Buy's Black Friday sale.&#160;</p><h2>Why should I shop at Best Buy instead of Amazon?</h2><p>There is one big benefit to shopping Best Buy over Amazon: its lower price guarantee. Best Buy says that if any qualifying item purchased during Best Buy's competing sale sees a lower price before November 28, the day after Black Friday, Best Buy will refund the difference.</p><p>Purchases made from Best Buy within the holiday time frame come with a much larger return window than the usual <a href=\"https://bestbuy.7tiv.net/c/196318/614286/10014?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bestbuy.com%2Fsite%2Fhelp-topics%2Freturn-exchange-policy%2Fpcmcat260800050014.c%3Fid%3Dpcmcat260800050014&subid2=1602501933080amrepvfzs&subId3=xid:fr1602501936312gdg36312gdg\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">15-day limit</a> the store typically offers. Purchases made between October 13 and January 2, 2021, can be returned through January 16, 2021. However, Amazon's return policy trumps this by a few weeks. On Amazon, purchases made during the same time period can be <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/?ots=1&slotNum=0&imprToken=aaba8e47-7a4f-154b-dfd&nodeId=GKM69DUUYKQWKWX7&_encoding=UTF8&tag=biipgf_072418_best-dog-dental-care-products-20&linkCode=ur2&linkId=013b0e9a818c3ed49e4748c4346617dd&camp=1789&creative=932517dd&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">returned until January 31, 2021</a>.</p><h2>Can I shop in the Best Buy near me?</h2><p>Shoppers can visit Best Buy locations to take advantage of these early Black Friday deals — a stark contrast to Amazon's online-only approach. The retailer is also rolling out new safety protocols for shopping in stores, including requiring customers and employees to wear face masks and limiting the number of visitors.</p><p>Additionally, homepage for more stories</a>.</strong></li></ul><p>The European Central Bank moved a step closer to exploring the creation of a virtual currency, after president Christine Lagarde said on Monday it was \"very seriously considering\" a digital euro.&#160;</p><p>At a virtual meeting hosted by the International Monetary Fund, Lagarde said: \"The ECB is very seriously looking at a digital Europe.\"&#160;</p><p>She said the COVID-19 pandemic has led to many structural changes including the way \"we work, we trade, and we pay.\"</p><p>Digital payments have increased significantly as a result, particularly in countries such as Germany and Italy where \"cash was king,\" Lagarde said.&#160;</p><p>\"People [used to] walk around with banknotes in [Germany and Italy],\" she said.&#160;</p><p>Lagarde said the pandemic caused e-commerce to rise by almost one fifth in terms of volumes and sales between February, when the outbreak first hit Europe, and June this year, when many of the toughest lockdown restrictions eased.&#160;</p><p>\"There is much more confidence in digital payments and significant change is underway,\" she added.&#160;</p><p>In a study published earlier this month, the ECB said a digital euro would <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/europe-must-prepare-issue-digital-euro-cash-ecb-panetta-says-2020-10-1029643193\">help citizens with access to quick money</a> in a fast-changing digital world.</p><p><strong data-stringify-type=\"bold\"><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\">Read more</em></strong><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\">:&#160;</em><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/investing-strategy-spac-etf-spak-benefits-risks-for-retail-investors-2020-10\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-stringify-link=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/investing-strategy-spac-etf-spak-benefits-risks-for-retail-investors-2020-10\" data-sk=\"tooltip_parent\">SPACs have generated a $39 billion frenzy in the US this year. The executive behind their first ETF explains how retail investors can use them to level the playing field with Wall Street titans like Warren Buffett.</a></em>&#160;</p><p>\"We should be ready to issue a digital euro if, and when, developments around us make it necessary,\" Fabio Panetta, member of the European Central Bank's executive board said in a <a href=\"https://www.ecb.europa.eu/press/blog/date/2020/html/ecb.blog201002~12ab1c06b5.en.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">blog post</a>&#160;related to the study. \"This means that we already need to be preparing for it.\"</p><p>The bank previously said the Eurosystem - the ECB and the national central banks that have adopted the euro - will take a decision by the middle of next year whether to go ahead with the proposal.&#160;</p><p>The Eurosystem will have to consider major concerns such as potential cyber risks, right to privacy, and whether a central bank introducing a digital currency means that it would acquire sensitive information on users.</p><p>It will also have to look into legal considerations such as the implications of different design features and the basis for issuance.</p><p>Lagarde said a digital euro would not replace cash, merely supplement it.&#160;</p><p>\"A digital euro will never be a substitute for cash. It is a very good supplement and a very good partial substitute for what was being done physically.\"</p><p>Cryptocurrencies such as Bitcoin, or Ethereum, have grown in popularity among traders and online shoppers. The total value of the crypto market has grown to around $360 billion this month, from around $175 billion just three years ago, according to data from <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/charts/\">CoinMarketCap.com</a>.</p><p><strong data-stringify-type=\"bold\"><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\">Read more</em></strong><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\">:&#160;</em><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/stock-picks-to-buy-companies-with-best-profit-growth-goldman-2020-10\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-stringify-link=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/stock-picks-to-buy-companies-with-best-profit-growth-goldman-2020-10\" data-sk=\"tooltip_parent\">GOLDMAN SACHS: Buy these 15 stocks set to deliver the strongest possible profit growth and subsequent returns through year-end</a></em></p><p>A number of central banks have started trialling digital payments.&#160;</p><p>The People's Bank of China began trial use of a digital yuan, currently the world's first digital currency backed by a central bank, in four major cities earlier this year, <a href=\"https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/apr/28/china-starts-major-trial-of-state-run-digital-currency#:~:text=China%20will%20begin%20trialling%20payments,operated%20by%20a%20major%20economy.\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">according to the Guardian</a>.&#160;</p><p>Sweden's Riksbank has been testing an&#160;<a href=\"https://www.riksbank.se/en-gb/payments--cash/e-krona/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">electronic form of the krona</a>&#160;for several months.</p><p>But other major central banks such as the Federal Reserve, the Bank of Japan, and the Bank of England have taken a more precious approach to the introduction of central bank-backed digital currencies.&#160;</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a 01:04:49","updatedTime":"2020-10-13 01:04:49","title":"Microsoft said it thwarted a sprawling network of bots that could have been used to target election infrastructure","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/microsoft-thwarts-massive-botnet-that-could-have-targeted-elections-2020-10","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f845812bab422001979abe8?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Election Day voting \" height=\"1378\" width=\"1837\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Stephen Maturen/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Microsoft announced Monday that it had taken action to significantly disrupt Trickbot, one of the most notorious bot networks that could have been used to target elections infrastructure.</li>\n<li>Trickbot was previously used to distribute ransomware, which experts and government officials warned posed a serious threat to elections and could have been used to target polling places' computer systems.</li>\n<li>Microsoft got permission from a federal court to take over the IP addresses associated with Trickbot's servers in order to quash the network, which the company said is a \"new legal approach.\"</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Microsoft has quashed a sprawling network of bots that could have been used to target voting infrastructure ahead of the Nov. 3 election, it <a href=\"https://blogs.microsoft.com/on-the-issues/2020/10/12/trickbot-ransomware-cyberthreat-us-elections/\">said</a> on Monday.</p><p>The company disrupted servers that were used to run Trickbot, a notorious botnet that has been used to deploy ransomware. Ransomware attacks against local governments have become increasingly common, and <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/2020/09/27/technology/2020-election-security-threats.html\">experts have warned</a> that a ransomware attack targeting elections offices could cause chaos on election day.</p><p>Microsoft said it was able to stamp out Trickbot after it obtained a court order granting permission to take control of the servers that hosted the botnet, and worked with telecom companies to quash the botnet. The action comes after the US military <a href=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/cyber-command-trickbot-disrupt/2020/10/09/19587aae-0a32-11eb-a166-dc429b380d10_story.html\">escalated its efforts</a> to take down Trickbot earlier this month.</p><p>\"We have now cut off key infrastructure so those operating Trickbot will no longer be able to initiate new infections or activate ransomware already dropped into computer systems,\" Microsoft vice president of security Tom Burt wrote in a <a href=\"https://blogs.microsoft.com/on-the-issues/2020/10/12/trickbot-ransomware-cyberthreat-us-elections/\">blog post</a> on the matter.</p><p>Trickbot had used malicious code to infect more than a million devices across the globe. The hackers behind the botnet would sell their services to other hackers, using the bots to deploy Ryuk ransomware that's used to take a target's computer systems offline until they agree to pay a ransom.</p><p>Last month, Ryuk was <a href=\"https://www.bleepingcomputer.com/news/security/uhs-hospitals-hit-by-reported-country-wide-ryuk-ransomware-attack/\">reportedly used</a> to take down the computer systems of Universal Health Services, one of the largest hospital chains in the US. The hack <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/uhs-cyberattack-hack-derails-surgeries-at-hospitals-across-us-2020-9\">took UHS' systems offline for nearly a week</a>, delaying surgeries and forcing staff to work with pen and paper.</p><p>In addition to ransomware, Trickbot has previously been used to spread misinformation and misleading phishing messages that aim to trick victims into thinking hackers are a trusted entity and handing over their personal information. Burt said Trickbot's spam campaigns have previously used messages about COVID-19 and Black Lives Matter protests to grab people's attention and get them to click on malicious links.</p><p>The botnet could eventually resurface despite Microsoft's action, but Burt said the company plans to pursue further court orders to preempt such a revival.</p><p>\"We fully anticipate Trickbot's operators will make efforts to revive their operations, and we will work with our partners to monitor their activities and take additional legal and technical steps to stop them,\" Burt said.</p><div 01:04:49","updatedTime":"2020-10-13 01:04:49","title":"'That product was cursed from the beginning' – the long, hard road to market for SoulCycle's 'Peloton killer'","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/soulcycle-equinox-home-bike-peltoton-trump-fundraiser-2020-10","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f809e754c3b2e0019bba351?format=jpeg\" alt=\"SoulCycle\" height=\"604\" width=\"805\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>SoulCycle&#39;s long-awaited home bike rolled out nationally this week.\n<p class=\"copyright\">SoulCycle</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>A national PR disaster, political protests, an internal tug-of-war, and executive resignations led up to SoulCycle's home bike rollout, sources said.</li>\n<li>The backstory of the home bike is a crash-course in what can go wrong with a product, current and former employees said in <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/soulcycle-scandal-ceo-melanie-whelan-spin-bullying-peloton-equinox-2020-9\">an exclusive story on the company's decline.</a></li>\n<li>The company pinned its hopes on a \"Peloton-killer,\" then battled parent company Equinox over control, delaying its release, sources said.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/soulcycle-scandal-ceo-melanie-whelan-spin-bullying-peloton-equinox-2020-9?r=soulcylce-peel\">You can read more about Soul Cycle's problems in our expos&#233;: \"After expensing $5,100 in Dior bags, SoulCycle's CEO was suddenly out. Now, an executive exodus and a culture war threaten to send the company off a cliff.\"</a></li>\n</ul><p>So many problems befell SoulCycle's at-home stationary bike, rolled out nationwide this week, that one former staffer told Business Insider, \"That product was cursed from the beginning.\"</p><p>A national PR disaster, political protests, dramatic internal tug-of-war, and executive resignations led up to <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.in/retail/news/soulcycle-rolls-out-at-home-bike-nationally-adding-new-unlimited-streaming-program-and-expanded-financing-options-for-riders/articleshow/78564002.cms\">the fitness company's announcement</a> that the internet-connected home bike is now widely available with unlimited streaming of its classes.</p><p>The backstory of the home bike is a crash-course in what can go wrong with product development and marketing, current and former employees of the boutique fitness brand told Business Insider in <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/soulcycle-scandal-ceo-melanie-whelan-spin-bullying-peloton-equinox-2020-9\">an exposé on the once high-flying company's decline.&#160;</a></p><p>The NYC company, which boomed nationally then watched new studios fail to lure riders, pinned its hopes on a \"Peloton-killer\" home bike to compete with its rival. Then SoulCycle battled parent company Equinox over control and branding of the product that delayed its release, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/soulcycle-scandal-ceo-melanie-whelan-spin-bullying-peloton-equinox-2020-9\">sources said.</a></p><p>As instructors bristled at pay cuts and corporate employees engaged in a culture war with Equinox during the first half of 2019, a home spin bike to challenge Peloton's provided a ray of hope, sources said.</p><p>\"SoulCycle was struggling to really innovate,\" one former senior employee said. \"The home bike was one attempt of many to try and reinvent SoulCycle.\" Many sources asked to remain anonymous for professional reasons. Their identities are known to Business Insider.</p><p>Employees said there was a major tech effort to create an internet-connected bike that could stream SoulCycle classes into riders' homes. SoulCycle executives believed the rival Peloton bike wasn't sturdy enough, its music wasn't prominent enough, and the experience was metrics-based, lacking SoulCycle's unique communal spirit that bred fiercely loyal customers.</p><p>On August 7, 2019, the day the bike was announced, news broke that Stephen Ross, the billionaire chairman of the Related Companies, which owns Equinox and SoulCycle, was&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/equinox-soulcycle-face-backlash-over-chairmans-trump-ties-2019-8\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"60\" data-uri=\"92c261729a695108d5a6b37a16b1b2fd\">hosting a fundraiser for President Donald Trump</a>&#160;at his Hamptons estate.</p><p>Many SoulCycle devotees&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/equinox-soulcycle-face-backlash-over-chairmans-trump-ties-2019-8\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"60\" data-uri=\"92c261729a695108d5a6b37a16b1b2fd\">felt betrayed</a>, with celebrities including&#160;<a href=\"https://twitter.com/chrissyteigen/status/1159192308077563904\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"60\" data-uri=\"5e4772ccbc469155f7511d92f144a325\">Chrissy Teigen calling for riders to quit</a>, and riders protesting outside studios.</p><p>\"The Trump fundraiser news breaking the day they announced the home bike was an omen of many bad things to come,\" a former high-ranking SoulCycle executive said.</p><p>A corporate tug-of-war over the home bike ensued. As the tech team finished work on the first big SoulCycle product to live beyond the studios, Equinox's rapacious financial eye narrowed on the target, employees said.</p><p>Equinox chief Harvey Spevak plucked the home bike from SoulCycle and dropped it into Equinox ownership. He wanted control of the new digital product so that Equinox could extend it across its various fitness companies, former employees said. Spevak declined to comment.&#160;</p><p>\"There was a lot of drama. We wanted to do it ourselves. We didn't want to sell it. It sold it for way below ask,\" the SoulCycle insider said, adding that it was ultimately purchased at cost, for about $10 million. (Equinox, a majority owner of SoulCycle, bought the intellectual property rights in order to compensate the other minority investors.)</p><p>Key members of the home-bike team, including chief technical officer Jeremy Landis, were irate, sources said. Morale plummeted as the team watched its work get swiped by a separate company for far below value. Landis declined to comment.</p><h2><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/soulcycle-scandal-ceo-melanie-whelan-spin-bullying-peloton-equinox-2020-9?r=soulcylce-peel\">Read more on SoulCycle's struggles in our exposé. \"</a><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/soulcycle-scandal-ceo-melanie-whelan-spin-bullying-peloton-equinox-2020-9?r=soulcylce-peel\">After expensing $5,100 in Dior bags, SoulCycle's CEO was suddenly out. Now, an executive exodus and a culture war threaten to send the company off a cliff.\"</a><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/soulcycle-scandal-ceo-melanie-whelan-spin-bullying-peloton-equinox-2020-9?r=soulcylce-peel\"></a></h2><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on
